  63. I used to run a tanning salon years ago and I've purchased for myself and others all kinds of premium tanning lotions, creams, accelerators, bronzers etc. This one isn't bad at all. It doesn't smell great but it doesn't smell awful either. The complaints by many about the smell is one that has to be looked at with some external variables not applicable to everyone. First of all, everybody's physiological makeup is different and this lotion will interact with an individual's body chemistry, which in itself promotes a distinctive odor, respective to each of us. Diet can also affect the way external cosmetic products smell when interacting with our sweat and scent glands. If someone drinks alcohol or eats pungent foods such as onion, garlic or curry, to name only a few; this will have an affect upon the way highly potent lotions such as \\"Black Storm\\" interact with an individual's skin and will play a determinant role in the development of any resulting body odor. Another way, in my opinion, to tell a good lotion of any kind, but especially tanning lotions, is to look at where \\"dimethicone\\" lies within the list of ingredients on the back of the bottle. It is second on Black Storm. Dimethicone protects and hydrates the skin. The one thing I am most pleased about regarding this lotion is its ease of use. That is to say, it is easy to apply evenly and it absorbs quickly. It is a great buy. The ingredients in the lotion seem to be the real deal and they aren't cheap. It has worked well for me so far and I recommend it for the moderate to serious tanner.
